        }
    }

    .spinner-border {
        --bs-spinner-width: 2rem;
        --bs-spinner-height: 2rem;
        --bs-spinner-vertical-align: -0.125em;

    }

    .spinner-border-sm {

    }

    @keyframes spinner-grow {
        0% {
            transform: scale(0);
        }

        50% {
            opacity: 1;
            transform: none;
        }
    }

    .spinner-grow {
        --bs-spinner-width: 2rem;
        --bs-spinner-height: 2rem;
